SOEC DNA MODEL  
 
C******************************************************************
**** 
      SUBROUTINE SOEC4 (KOMTY,ANTLK,ANTEX,ANTKN,ANTPK,ANTM1, 
     $     MEDIE,ANTME,VARME,ANTEL,VAREL,parnam,zanam 
     $     ,MDOT,P,H,E,Q,ZA,PAR,RES,X_J,KOMDSC,KMEDDS,K_PAR,K_LIG 
     $     ,K_BET,k_inp) 
C******************************************************************
**** 
C  SOEC4 is a model of an solid oxyde electrolyzer cell based on 
the  
c SOFCEQ_1DN2 and the equations found in Akikur 2014 "Performance 
analysis 
c of a cogeneration system using solar energy and SOFC technology" 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
CA FKOMP - INPUT  - Flag with the value: 
CA                     1: Initialize the component. 
CA                     2: Initialize with actual system. 
CA                     3: Fluid composition calculation (constant). 
CA                     4: Find residuals. 
CA                     5: Find residuals and check variables. 
CA                     6: Output information about component. 
C 
CA KOMTY - OUTPUT - Component name. 
CA ANTLK - OUTPUT - Number of equations in the component. 
CA ANTEX - OUTPUT - Number of independent equations in the 
component. 
CA ANTKN - OUTPUT - Number of nodes connected to the component. 
CA ANTPK - OUTPUT - Number of parameters for the component. 
CA ANTM1 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the first conservation 
of 
CA                  mass equation. 
CA MEDIE - IN/OUT - Media (fluid) of the connected nodes. 
CA                  The values mean : 
CA                     -4    : Any gas 
CA ANTME - OUTPUT - Number of fluids with variable composition. 
CA VARME - OUTPUT - Pointer to fluid numbers (with variable 
composition). 
CA ANTEL - OUTPUT - Number of computed compounds in these variable 
fluids. 
CA VAREL - OUTPUT - Compound numbers in variable fluids. 
CA PARNAM- OUTPUT - Parameter Names 
CA ZANAM - OUTPUT - Additional Algebraic Variable Names 
CA MDOT  - INPUT  - Massflows from nodes. 
CA P     - INPUT  - Pressure in nodes. 
CA H     - INPUT  - Enthalpy 
CA E     - INPUT  - Elecrical power 
CA Q     - INPUT  - Heat 
CA ZA    - INPUT  - Algebraic Variable 
CA PAR   - OUTPUT - Parameter 
==PAGE:102==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
101 
 
CA RES   - OUTPUT - Residuals for the component. 
CA X_J   - INPUT  - Fluid composition. 
CA KOMDES- OUTPUT - Component description. 
CA KMEDDS- OUTPUT - Media Desciption 
CL K_PAR - OUTPUT - Parameter description. 
CL K_LIG - OUTPUT - Equation description. 
CL K_BET - OUTPUT - Condition description. 
CL K_INP - OUTPUT - Input description 
C 
C  Subroutines : COMINF 
C 
CP Programmer : Nicolas Cobos Ullvius 2015  
CP              Thermal Energy syetems, DTU, Denmark. 
C                 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C  Including the common "environment" 
C 
      INCLUDE 'ENVIRO.INI' 
      INCLUDE 'THERPROP.DEC' 
      INCLUDE 'GASI.DEC' 
C 
C  Parameter variables 
C 
      INTEGER           ANTLK, ANTEX, ANTKN, MEDIE(5), ANTPK, 
     :                  ANTM1, ANTME, VARME(4), ANTEL(3), 
     :                  VAREL(ANTST,2) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  X_J(MAXME,ANTST), RES(26), MDOT(3), 
P(3),H(3), 
     :                  E,Q,PAR(4),ZA(10) 
      CHARACTER*3       DYCOM(5) 
      CHARACTER*80      KOMTY,PARNAM(8),ZANAM(20) 
C 
C  Local variables 
 
C 
      INTEGER I 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  NIN(100),NOUT(100),EACT,ECONC,ENERNST, 
     $     EOHM,EOTHER,G(7),HG(6),R,M_BR_OUT,M_AIR_OUT, T2, T3, 
     $     ETAPRO, U, V, S, X, DUM,M_BL(4), NO2IN, 
NH2IN,DP1,DP2,PGAS, 
     $     TGAS,ETAMAX,T0,GMAX,NOS,CPS,WMOD,IDENS,STCR,lAN,LCA,LEL, 
     $     
ACELL,P0,PH2,PO2,PH2O,UF,F,EPOL,ECELL,RAN,RCA,REL,ESTACK,  
     $     
ALPHA,ALPHAA,ALPHAB,I0,I0A,I0B,I0C,UPPER,LOWER,GUESS,USERRES, 
     $     
EACT2,COUNT,CURR,LHV,KLOSS,DP,NH2OUSED,ECELLF,UPPER2,LOWER2, 
     $     GUESS2,USERRES2,COUNT2,J,qr,E0 
      DOUBLE PRECISION rp,k,tor,por,Ac,Bc,Cc,Dc,Ec,Fc,Gc,Hc,D_H2Ok, 
     $     MH2H2O,SGM_H2,SGM_H2O,SGM_H2H2O,epsi,tau,OMG_D,D_H2H2O, 
     $     
DH2O_EFF,ECONC2,atmPa,ECONC_AN,ECONC_CA,D_O2k,DO2_EFF,ICS, 
     $     D_H2H2OEFF,D_H2OkEFF,B_g,mu_O2,KK,Pr,ECONC_AN2 
      CHARACTER*100      K_PAR(5) 
      CHARACTER*500      K_LIG(20), K_BET, KOMDSC,K_INP 
      CHARACTER*100      KMEDDS(6) 
==PAGE:103==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
102 
 
      EXTERNAL          COMINF 
      INCLUDE 'THERPROP.INI' 
      INCLUDE 'GASI.INI' 
 
C==================================================================
===== 
      GOTO (200,200,1,400,400,200) FKOMP 
 1    RETURN 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component name 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
c  100 CONTINUE 
c      KOMTY    = 'SOEC4' 
c      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component characteristics 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  200 CONTINUE 
      KOMTY    = 'SOEC4' 
C Number of nodes 
      ANTKN    =  5 
C Number of parameters 
      ANTPK    =  4 
C Number of equations excluding ZA's 
      ANTLK    =  7 
C Number of ZA'S 
      ANTEX    =  9 
 
      ANTM1    =  3 
      MEDIE(1) =  anygas$ 
      ANTEL(1) =  0 
      MEDIE(2) =  anygas$ 
      ANTEL(2) =  2 
      MEDIE(3) =  anygas$ 
      ANTEL(3) =  0 
      MEDIE(4) =  power$ 
      MEDIE(5) =  heat$ 
      ANTME    =  3 
      VARME(1) =  NODE1$ 
      VARME(2) =  NODE2$ 
      VARME(3) =  NODE3$ 
      VAREL(1,2)=H2$ 
      VAREL(2,2)=H2O_G$ 
      ZANAM(1) = 'ECELL' 
      ZANAM(2) = 'EPOL' 
      ZANAM(3) = 'EOHM' 
      ZANAM(4) = 'ECONC' 
      ZANAM(5) = 'EACT' 
      ZANAM(6) = 'J' 
      ZANAM(7) = 'H2 PROD KG/S' 
      ZANAM(8) = 'EFF EL' 
      ZANAM(9) = 'XJ H2 OUT' 
       
      PARNAM(1) = 'TGAS' 
==PAGE:104==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
103 
 
      PARNAM(2) = 'DP FUEL' 
      PARNAM(3) = 'CELL PR STACK' 
      PARNAM(4) = 'NUMBER OF STACKS' 
 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.6) GOTO 600 
***   FKOMP = 3 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component equations. All in residual form. 
C  Do not include the conservation laws, since these are treated 
C  automatically by DNA. 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  400 CONTINUE 
       
 
      TGAS=PAR(1) 
      DP=PAR(2) 
      CPS=PAR(3) 
      NOS=PAR(4) 
 
 
 
C     Constants 
      R    = 8.314D0 
      T0   = 298.15D0 
      PGAS = P(3) 
      P0   = 1.01325 
 
C   Faradays constant [C/mol] 
      F=9.64867D4 
 
C Cell area 
      ACELL=0.12**2 
 
C     Thickness of the different parts of the cell in meters 
C      LAN=600.0D-6 
C      LCA=50.0D-6 
C      LEL=10.0D-6 
      LCA=600.0D-6 
      LAN=50.0D-6 
      LEL=10.0D-6 
 
 
 
C PRESSURE DROP 
      RES(1)=P(1)*(1-DP)-P(2) 
      RES(2)=P(2)-P(3) 
 
C OUTLET TEMPERATURE 
      CALL STATES(P(2),H(2),T2,V,S,X,DUM,1,2,MEDIE(2)) 
      CALL STATES(P(3),H(3),T3,V,S,X,DUM,1,2,MEDIE(3))    
      RES(3)=T2-TGAS 
      RES(4)=T3-TGAS 
 
C OUTLET COMPOSITION 
 
==PAGE:105==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
104 
 
C     Molar mass of the gases 
      M_BL(1)=0.D0 
      M_BL(2)=0.D0 
      M_BL(3)=0.D0 
      DO I=1,ANTST 
        M_BL(1)=X_J(MEDIE(1),I)*M_MOL(I)+M_BL(1) 
        M_BL(2)=X_J(MEDIE(2),I)*M_MOL(I)+M_BL(2) 
        M_BL(3)=X_J(MEDIE(3),I)*M_MOL(I)+M_BL(3) 
      ENDDO 
c      WRITE(6,*)'M_BL(1) ',M_BL(1) 
c      WRITE(6,*)'M_BL(2) ',M_BL(2) 
c      WRITE(6,*)'M_BL(3) ',M_BL(3) 
 
 
C  Calculate mole flow of each species in to the reaction 
      DO I=1,ANTST 
        NIN(I)=MDOT(1)*X_J(MEDIE(1),I)/M_BL(1)  
      ENDDO 
c      WRITE(6,*)'NIN(H2O_G$) ',NIN(H2O_G$) 
 
 
 
      
      COUNT2=0 
      ECELL=ZA(1) 
      WMOD = E 
c      WRITE(6,*)'WMOD ',WMOD 
 
 
c Start iteration method to calculate the cell voltage and current 
knowing 
c the power input. 
      DO I=1,50 
         COUNT2=COUNT2+1 
c         WRITE(6,*)'COUNT2 ',COUNT2 
C         GUESS2=(UPPER+LOWER)/2 
         ECELLF=ECELL 
 
 
 
c Voltage produced by each stack 
         ESTACK=ECELLF*CPS 
 
C  Current density [A/m2] 
         J=WMOD*1000/(ESTACK*ACELL*NOS) 
c         WRITE(6,*)'WMOD ',WMOD 
c         WRITE(6,*)'J ',J 
 
 
 
         NH2OUSED = NOS*CPS*J*ACELL/(2*F*1D3) 
c         WRITE(6,*)'NH2OUSED ',NH2OUSED 
 
 
C Composition of air node 4 kmol/s      
         RES(5) = MDOT(3)/M_BL(3)*X_J(MEDIE(3),O2$)+NH2OUSED/2   
 
 
==PAGE:106==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
105 
 
C  Hydrogen concentration outlet, node 3 (kmol/s) 
         RES(6)= MDOT(2)/M_BL(2)*X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$)+ 
     $        NH2OUSED+ 
     $        MDOT(1)/M_BL(1)*X_J(MEDIE(1),H2$) 
 
         RES(7)=1.d0-X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$)-X_J(MEDIE(2),H2O_G$) 
 
c      WRITE(6,*)'H2O OUT ',MDOT(2)/M_BL(2)*X_J(MEDIE(2),H2O_G$) 
c      WRITE(6,*)'H2 OUT ',MDOT(2)/M_BL(2)*X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$) 
 
 
 
 
C  Gibbs' free energy of each compound 
          
         CALL STATES(P(2),H(2),TGAS,V,S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(2)) 
         TGAS = TGAS+273.15D0 
         CALL GIBBS(H2$,TGAS,P(2),G(1)) 
         CALL GIBBS(H2O_G$,TGAS,P(2),G(2)) 
         CALL GIBBS(O2$,TGAS,P(3),G(3)) 
  
 
 
C     Electrochemical calculations 
 
 
 
    
C   Calculation of partial pressures     
         PH2=X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$)*P(2)/P0 
         PH2O=X_J(MEDIE(2),H2O_G$)*P(2)/P0 
         PO2=X_J(MEDIE(3),O2$)*P(3)/P0 
          
         IF(PH2.LE.0) THEN 
            ENERNST=0 
         ELSE IF(PH2O.LE.0) THEN 
            ENERNST=0 
         ELSE IF(PO2.LE.0) THEN 
            ENERNST=0 
         ELSE              
            ENERNST = -(G(2)-(0.5*G(3)+G(1)))/(2*F) 
     $           -((R*TGAS/(2*F))*DLOG(PH2O/(PH2*DSQRT(PO2))))     
         ENDIF 
 
         E0=-(G(2)-(0.5*G(3)+G(1)))/(2*F) 
C          WRITE(6,*)'ENERNST ',ENERNST 
C          WRITE(6,*)'E0 ',E0 
C Polarizations 
 
C "Other losses": Leaks, contact resistsance etc.; assumed constant 
         EOTHER = 0.06 
          
C Actication polarization 
         ALPHAA=0.00129113645402 
         ALPHAB=-0.85816436773410 
         ALPHA=ALPHAA*TGAS+ALPHAB 
         I0A=9.99999996139714 
         I0B=-8.750938523270041E003 
==PAGE:107==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
106 
 
         I0C=4.601660702742138E003 
         I0=(I0A*TGAS+I0B)*DEXP(I0C/(TGAS*R)) 
C         CALL  DEACT2(EACT,IDENS,TGAS) 
       
C     Parameters for bisection root finding 
         USERRES=1 
         UPPER=1 
         LOWER=-1 
         COUNT=0 
     
         DO WHILE(ABS(USERRES).GE.1E-6) 
            COUNT=COUNT+1 
             
            GUESS=(UPPER+LOWER)/2 
            USERRES=I0*(DEXP((2*ALPHA*F)/(R*TGAS)*GUESS)-DEXP((-2* 
     $           (1-ALPHA)*F)/(R*TGAS)*GUESS))-J 
          
            IF(USERRES.GE.0) THEN 
               UPPER=GUESS 
            ELSE 
               LOWER=GUESS 
            END IF 
            EACT=GUESS 
         END DO 
c      print *,EACT  
      
C Ohmic polarization 
         call ROHM(2,LAN,RAN,TGAS) 
         call ROHM(1,LCA,RCA,TGAS) 
         call ROHM(3,LEL,REL,TGAS) 
         EOHM = (RAN+RCA+REL)*J 
 
           
         TGAS = TGAS+273.15D0 
C 
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
///// 
C Concentration polarization 
c tortuosity and porosity 
         tor=2.5 
         por=0.3 
c pore radius 
         rp=(0.5D-6)/0.4*por 
 
         k=1.38066D-23 
c          WRITE(6,*)'rp',rp 
C          WRITE(6,*)'TGAS',TGAS 
c           WRITE(6,*)'M_MOL(H2O_G$)',M_MOL(H2O_G$) 
c           WRITE(6,*)'R',R 
 
 
c Effective diffusion of H2O to H2 
C//////////////////DEFFH2O//////////////////////// 
           qr=(8000*R*TGAS/(M_MOL(H2O_G$)*3.14159))**0.5 
         D_H2Ok=2*rp*qr/3 
c           D_H2Ok=97*rp*(TGAS/M_MOL(H2O_G$))**0.5 
         D_H2OkEFF=(por/tor)*D_H2Ok 
         MH2H2O=2*(1/M_MOL(H2$)+1/M_MOL(H2O_G$))**(-1) 
==PAGE:108==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
107 
 
c         WRITE(6,*)'MH2H2O',MH2H2O 
         SGM_H2=2.827 
         SGM_H2O=2.641 
         SGM_H2H2O=(SGM_H2+SGM_H2O)/2 
c         WRITE(6,*)'SGM_H2H2O',SGM_H2H2O 
 
         epsi=(809.1*k*59.7*k)**0.5 
         tau=k*TGAS/epsi 
c         WRITE(6,*)'TAU',tau 
         Ac=1.06036 
         Bc=0.15610 
         Cc=0.19300 
         Dc=0.47635 
         Ec=1.03587 
         Fc=1.52996  
         Gc=1.76474 
         Hc=3.89411 
         
OMG_D=Ac/(tau**Bc)+Cc/exp(Dc*tau)+Ec/exp(Fc*tau)+Gc/(Hc*tau) 
c          WRITE(6,*)'OMG_D',OMG_D 
 
         D_H2H2O=((0.0026*TGAS**1.5)/ 
     $        (P(2)*(MH2H2O**0.5)*(SGM_H2H2O**2)*OMG_D))/10000 
         D_H2H2OEFF=D_H2H2O*(por/tor) 
 
         DH2O_EFF=1/((tor/por)*(1/D_H2Ok+1/D_H2H2O)) 
 
C         WRITE(6,*)'DH2O_EFF',DH2O_EFF 
C         WRITE(6,*)'D_H2H2O',D_H2H2O 
C         WRITE(6,*)'D_H2Ok',D_H2Ok 
 
 
c Effective diffusion of O2 
C/////////////// DEFF O2 /////////////////// 
 
          qr=(8000*R*TGAS/(M_MOL(O2$)*3.14159))**0.5 
         D_O2k=2*rp*qr/3 
c           D_H2Ok=97*rp*(TGAS/M_MOL(O2$))**0.5 
 
         DO2_EFF=(por/tor)*D_O2k 
 
C         WRITE(6,*)'DO2_EFF',DO2_EFF 
 
 
         atmPa=1.0133D5 
 
 
         ECONC_CA=R*TGAS/(2*F)* 
     $        DLOG((1+(J*R*TGAS*LCA)/(2*F*DH2O_EFF*PH2*atmPa))/ 
     $        (1-(J*R*TGAS*LCA)/(2*F*DH2O_EFF*PH2O*atmPa))) 
 
 
c Control of the limiting current 
C                  WRITE(6,*)'ECONC_CA',ECONC_CA 
C         ICS=(2*F*DH2O_EFF*PH2*atmPa)/(R*TGAS*LCA) 
C         WRITE(6,*)'LIMIT CURRENT CAT',ICS 
C         ICS=(2*F*DH2O_EFF*PH2O*atmPa)/(R*TGAS*LCA) 
C         WRITE(6,*)'LIMIT CURRENT CAT',ICS 
==PAGE:109==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
108 
 
 
c Concentration polarization in the Oxygen side 
c         CALL STATES(P(3),H(3),T3,V,S,X,DUM,1,2,MEDIE(3)) 
c         call TRAPRO(mu_O2,KK,Pr,P(3),T3,V,X,MEDIE(3),0) 
c         WRITE(6,*)'mu_O2',mu_O2 
c         B_g=por**3*(2*0.5E-6)**2/(72*tor*(1-por)**2) 
c         WRITE(6,*)'B_g',B_g 
 
 
  
c        methode 1          
c         ECONC_AN2=R*TGAS/(4*F)* 
c     $        
DLOG(DSQRT((PO2*atmPa)**2+(J*R*TGAS*mu_O2*LAN/(2*F*B_g)))/ 
c     $        (atmPa*PO2)) 
c         WRITE(6,*)'ECONC_AN2',ECONC_AN2 
 
 
c       methode 2 
c         ECONC_AN=(R*TGAS/(2*F))* 
c     $        
DLOG((1+(R*TGAS*J*LAN)/(DO2_EFF*PO2*atmPa*4*F))**0.5) 
c                  WRITE(6,*)'ECONC_AN',ECONC_AN 
 
  
 
 
c Concentration of polarization 
 
c         ECONC=ECONC_AN+ECONC_CA 
         ECONC=ECONC_CA 
c         WRITE(6,*)'ECONC',ECONC 
 
C          CALL DECONC2(ECONC2,J,LCA,P(2),TGAS,X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$) 
C     $     ,X_J(MEDIE(2),H2O_G$)) 
C         WRITE(6,*)'ECONC2',ECONC2 
          
C 
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
////// 
C The total polarization is the sum of the above contributions 
         EPOL = EACT+EOHM+ECONC+EOTHER 
c         WRITE(6,*)'EPOL ',EPOL 
 
C Calculating resulting cell voltage 
         IF(EACT.LE.0) THEN 
            ECELL = 0 
         ELSE IF(ECONC.LE.0) THEN  
            ECELL = 0 
         ELSE 
            ECELL = ENERNST+EPOL 
         ENDIF      
  
 
c         WRITE(6,*)'ECELL ',ECELL 
 
 
         USERRES2=ECELLF-ECELL 
==PAGE:110==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
109 
 
C         WRITE(6,*)'USERRES2',USERRES2 
 
      ENDDO 
c End of the iteration 
 
c Lower heating value of Hydrogen 
      LHV=242000 
 
 
c extra results    
      RES(8)= ZA(1)-ECELL 
      RES(9)= ZA(2)-EPOL 
      RES(10)= ZA(3)-EOHM 
      RES(11)= ZA(4)-ECONC 
      RES(12)= ZA(5)-EACT 
      RES(13)= ZA(6)-J 
      RES(14)= ZA(7)-NH2OUSED*M_MOL(H2$) 
       
      IF (Q.GT.1D-10)THEN 
      RES(15)= ZA(8)-(NH2OUSED*LHV)/(E+Q) 
      ELSE 
      RES(15)= ZA(8)-(NH2OUSED*LHV)/E 
      ENDIF 
 
      RES(16) = ZA(9) - X_J(MEDIE(2),H2$) 
 
 
 
       IF (FKOMP.EQ.5) GOTO 500 
       GOTO 9999 
        
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Solution check 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  500 CONTINUE 
      IF (MDOT(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(2).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(3).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
       
C      DO I=1,ANTST 
C        PRINT*,X_J(MEDIE(3),I),X_J(MEDIE(4),I) 
C      ENDDO 
      GOTO 9999 
  550 FBETI = .FALSE. 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Write component information 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  600 CONTINUE 
      KOMDSC = 'Fuel cell with given Hydrogen utilization and '// 
     $     'efficiency. Composition of the depleted fuel is '// 
     $     'calculated by chemical equilibrium.¤' 
      K_PAR(1) = 'Hydrogen utilization: $\alpha$  [--]¤' 
      K_PAR(2) = 'Cell efficiency: $\\eta_{cell}$ [--]¤' 
==PAGE:111==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
110 
 
      K_PAR(3) = 'Operating temperature: $T_{cell}$ [\\degC]¤' 
      K_PAR(4) = 'Fractional pressure loss fuel: $\\beta_{13}$ [--
]¤' 
      K_PAR(5) = 'Fractional pressure loss air: $\\beta_{24}$ [--
]¤' 
      K_LIG(1) = 'Pressure loss fuel: $p_3=p_1(1-\\beta_{13})$¤' 
      K_LIG(2) = 'Pressure loss air: $p_4=p_2(1-\\beta_{24})$¤' 
      K_LIG(3) = 'Temperature of outlet fuel: $T_3=T_{cell}$¤' 
      K_LIG(4) = 'Temperature of outlet air: $T_4=T_3$¤' 
      K_LIG(5) = 'Mass flow of used air: '// 
     $     '$\\dot{m}_4=\\dot{m_2}-'// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{O_2,actual}}M_{\\mathrm{O_2}}$¤' 
      K_LIG(6) = 'Oxygen balance on air side: '// 
     $     '$\\frac{\\dot{m}_4}{M_4}y_{\\mathrm{O_2},4}='// 
     $     '\\frac{\\dot{m_2}}{M_2}y_{\\mathrm{O_2},2}-'// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{O_2,actual}}$¤' 
      K_LIG(7) = 'Nitrogen balance on air side: '// 
     $     '$\\frac{\\dot{m}_4}{M_4}y_{\\mathrm{N_2},4}='// 
     $     '\\frac{\\dot{m_2}}{M_2}y_{\\mathrm{N_2},2}$¤' 
      K_LIG(8) = 'Carbon Dioxide balance on air side: '// 
     $     '$\\frac{\\dot{m}_4}{M_4}y_{\\mathrm{CO_2},4}='// 
     $     '\\frac{\\dot{m_2}}{M_2}y_{\\mathrm{CO_2},2}$¤' 
      K_LIG(9) = 'Water balance on air side: '// 
     $     '$\\frac{\\dot{m}_4}{M_4}y_{\\mathrm{H_2O},4}='// 
     $     '\\frac{\\dot{m_2}}{M_2}y_{\\mathrm{H_2O},2}$¤' 
      K_LIG(10) = 'Summation of molar fractions of used air: '// 
     $     '$y_{\\mathrm{O_2},4}+y_{\\mathrm{N_2},4}+'// 
     $     'y_{\\mathrm{CO_2},4}+y_{\\mathrm{H_2O},4}+'// 
     $     'y_{\\mathrm{Ar},4}=1$¤' 
      K_LIG(11) = 'Partial derivative of Gibbs energy of outlet '// 
     $     'gas with respect to Hydrogen content of gas:'// 
     $     '$$\\frac{\\partial F}{\\partial '// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{H_2,out}}}='// 
     $     '\\frac{g_{\\mathrm{H_2,out}}^0}{RT}+'// 
     $     '\\ln(y_{\\mathrm{H_2,out}}p_3)+'// 
     $     '\\sum_{j\\mathrm{ in H,C,O}}'// 
     $     '\\mu_j \\mathbf{A}_{\\mathrm{H_2},j}$$, '// 
     $     'where $\\mathbf{A}$ is a matrix with information on 
the'// 
     $     ' moles of $j$ in each mole $\\mathrm{H_2}$. ¤' 
      K_LIG(12) = 'Partial derivative of Gibbs energy of outlet '// 
     $     'gas with respect to Carbon Monoxide content of gas:'// 
     $     '$$\\frac{\\partial F}{\\partial '// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{CO,out}}}='// 
     $     '\\frac{g_{\\mathrm{CO,out}}^0}{RT}+'// 
     $     '\\ln(y_{\\mathrm{CO,out}}p_3)+'// 
     $     '\\sum_{j\\mathrm{ in H,C,O}}'// 
     $     '\\mu_j \\mathbf{A}_{\\mathrm{CO},j}$$, '// 
     $     'where $\\mathbf{A}$ is a matrix with information on 
the'// 
     $     ' moles of $j$ in each mole $\\mathrm{CO}$. ¤' 
      K_LIG(13) = 'Partial derivative of Gibbs energy of outlet '// 
     $     'gas with respect to Carbon Dioxide content of gas:'// 
     $     '$$\\frac{\\partial F}'// 
     $     '{\\partial \\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{CO_2,out}}}='// 
     $     '\\frac{g_{\\mathrm{CO_2,out}}^0}{RT}+'// 
     $     '\\ln(y_{\\mathrm{CO_2,out}}p_3)+'// 
     $     '\\sum_{j\\mathrm{ in H,C,O}}'// 
==PAGE:112==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
111 
 
     $     '\\mu_j \\mathbf{A}_{\\mathrm{CO_2},j}$$, '// 
     $     'where $\\mathbf{A}$ is a matrix with information on 
the'// 
     $     ' moles of $j$ in each mole $\\mathrm{CO_2}$. ¤' 
      K_LIG(14) = 'Partial derivative of Gibbs energy of outlet '// 
     $     'gas with respect to water content of gas:'// 
     $     '$$\\frac{\\partial F}'// 
     $     '{\\partial \\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{H_2O,out}}}='// 
     $     '\\frac{g_{\\mathrm{H_2O,out}}^0}{RT}+'// 
     $     '\\ln(y_{\\mathrm{H_2O,out}}p_3)+'//

     $     'where $\\mathbf{A}$ is a matrix with information on 
the'//

      K_LIG(15) = 'Partial derivative of Gibbs energy of outlet '// 
     $     'gas with respect to methane content of gas:'// 
     $     '$$\\frac{\\partial F}'// 
     $     '{\\partial \\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{CH_4,out}}}='//

     $     '\\ln(y_{\\mathrm{CH_4,out}}p_3)+'// 
     $     '\\sum_{j\\mathrm{ in H,C,O}}'//

     $     'where $\\mathbf{A}$ is a matrix with information on 
the'// 
     $     ' moles of $j$ in each mole $\\mathrm{CH_4}$. ¤' 
      K_LIG(16) = 'Molar balance for Hydrogen: '// 
     $     '$\\sum_{i \\mathrm{ in inlet gas}}'//

      K_LIG(17) = 'Molar balance for Carbon: '//

'//

      K_LIG(18) = 'Molar balance for Oxygen: '// 
     $     '$\\sum_{i \\mathrm{ in inlet gas}}'// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_{i,\\mathrm{in}}\\mathbf{A}_{i,\\mathrm{O}}-
'// 
     $     '\\sum_{i \\mathrm{ in outlet gas}}'// 
     $     
'\\dot{n}_{i,\\mathrm{out}}\\mathbf{A}_{i,\\mathrm{O}}$¤' 
      K_LIG(19) = 'Gibbs energy of depleted fuel:'// 
     $     '$G = \\sum_{i \\mathrm{in outlet gas}} '// 
     $     '\\dot{n}_i \\left( g_i^0 + R T \\ln{y_ip} \\right)$¤' 
      K_LIG(20) = 'Power production: '// 
     $     '$\\dot{E}=\\eta_{max}\\eta_{cell}\\alpha'// 
     $     '\\sum_{i \\mathrm{in fuel}} H_u,i$, where '// 
     $     '$\\alpha=\\frac{\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{H_2,cons}}}'// 
     $     '{\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{H_2}}+\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{CO}}'// 
     $     '+4\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{CH_4}}}$¤' 
      K_BET = '$\\dot{m}_1 \\gt 0 $\\\\$\\dot{m}_2 \\gt 0 $\\\\'// 
     $     '$\\dot{m}_3 \\gt 0 $\\\\$\\dot{m}_4 \\gt 0 $¤'

      KMEDDS(1) = 'Fuel inlet¤' 
      KMEDDS(2) = 'Air inlet¤' 
      KMEDDS(3) = 'Depleted fuel out¤' 
      KMEDDS(4) = 'Used air out¤' 
      KMEDDS(5) = 'Power¤' 
      KMEDDS(6) = 'Heat loss¤' 
      K_INP='struc sofc sofceq_1 1 2 3 4 201 301 1 '// 
     $     '1 1000 0.1 0.1\\\\'// 
     $     'fluid fuel H2 0.99 CO2 0.01\\\\'//

     $     't sofc 2 700 p 2 3\\\\'//

     $     'varpa sofc 3 m sofc 2 30¤' 
      GOTO 9999

 9999 CONTINUE 
      RETURN 
      END

==PAGE:114==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
113 
 
 
DISH STIRLING DNA MODEL 
NOTE: only Stirling_2 is shown because the other one is very similar. 
 
 
C******************************************************************
***** 
      SUBROUTINE 
STIRLING_2(KOMTY,ANTLK,ANTEX,ANTKN,ANTPK,ANTM1,ANTM2,   
     :                      
MEDIE,ANTME,VARME,ANTEL,VAREL,MDOT,E,P,H,Q, 
     :                      PAR,RES,X_J,ZA,ZANAM) 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C  Stirling_2 is a simple model of a Dish concentrator-stirling 
engine system. 
c It is made based on Stirling_1 but in this case, the heat 
supplied depends 
c mainly on the parameter Irradiation. Data is taken from Richard 
B. Diver, 1994 
c " A compendium of solar dish/stirling technology" 
 
c In this model, the power node has to be specified and it will 
represent the 
c demand to cover. The extra power is shown in the extra results. 
C 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
CA FKOMP - INPUT  - Flag with the value: 
CA                     1: Initialize the component. 
CA                     2: Initialize with actual system. 
CA                     3: Fluid composition calculation (constant). 
CA                     4: Find residuals. 
CA                     5: Find residuals and check variables. 
CA                     6: Output information about component. 
CA MDOT  - INPUT  - Massflows from nodes. 
CA P     - INPUT  - Pressure in nodes. 
CA Q     - INPUT  - Exchanged heat. 
CA PAR   - INPUT  - Parameters of the component. 
CA X_J   - INPUT  - Fluid composition. 
CA KOMTY - OUTPUT - Component name. 
CA ANTPK - OUTPUT - Number of parameters for the component. 
CA ANTLK - OUTPUT - Number of equations in the component. 
CA ANTEX - OUTPUT - Number of independent equations in the 
component. 
CA ANTED - OUTPUT - Number of differential independent equations. 
CA ANTKN - OUTPUT - Number of nodes connected to the component. 
CA ANTM1 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the first conservation 
of 
CA                  mass equation. 
CA ANTM2 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the second. 
==PAGE:115==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
114 
 
CA DYCOM - OUTPUT - Type of conservation equations (static or 
dynamic 
CA                  mass and internal energy on side 1 and 2 
respectively; 
CA                  and dynamic solid internal energy). 
CA MEDIE - IN/OUT - Media (fluid) of the connected nodes. 
CA                  The values mean : 
CA                     29    : Nitrogen rich gas. 
CA                     26    : Syngas. 
CA                     31    : Exhaust gas (variable composition). 
CA                     300   : Heat. 
CA ANTME - OUTPUT - Number of fluids with variable composition. 
CA VARME - OUTPUT - Fluid numbers (with variable composition). 
CA ANTEL - OUTPUT - Number of compounds in these variable fluids. 
CA VAREL - OUTPUT - Compound numbers in variable fluids. 
CA RES   - OUTPUT - Residuals for the component. 
C 
CL AF    Nitrogen rich air-to-syngas ratio. 
CL DPP   P3 as a percentage of P1. 
CL XPRO  Exhaust gas composition. 
CL K_PAR Parameter description. 
CL K_LIG Equation description. 
CL K_BET Condition description. 
CL K_MED Media description. 
C 
C  Subroutines : COMB_PRO 
C                COMINF 
 
CP Programmer : Nicolás Cobos Ullvius 2015 
CP              Thermal Energy, DTU, Denmark. 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C  Including the common "environment" 
C 
      INCLUDE 'ENVIRO.INI' 
      INCLUDE 'THERPROP.DEC' 
C 
C  Parameter variables 
C 
      INTEGER           ANTEX,ANTLK, ANTKN, MEDIE(7), ANTPK, 
     :                  ANTM1,ANTM2, ANTME, VARME(5), ANTEL(8), 
     :                  VAREL(ANTST,3) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  X_J(MAXME,ANTST), 
PAR(13),RES(COMRES),MDOT(5), 
     :                  P(5),Q(3),E,U,S,X,ZA(COMZA) 
      CHARACTER*20      KOMTY 
C 
C  Local variables 
C 
      INTEGER           K_MED(7) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  DPP_HEAT,DPP_COOL,EPSILON1,EPSILON2  
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
etamech,etapcy,gamma,DELTAT_LOW,DELTAT_HIGH,H2 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
QLOSS,QHIGH,QLOW,POWER,T_COOLERGAS,T_COOLERWALL 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
T_HEATERGAS,T_HEATERWALL,RV,T_WATERIN,T_WATEROUT 
==PAGE:116==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
115 
 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  T_FGIN,T_FGOUT,V(4),H(4),zeta,XPRO(ANTST) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
V_w,T_sky,T_a,U_supp_ratio,N_UNITS,power_2grid 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
D_abs,Re_w,Nu_w,h_w,U_cc,Tracking_power_pu,IRR 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
D,C,BOLTZ,PI,A_col,APP_TOTAL,CONC_EFF,EFF_total 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
abs,transmit,REC_EFF,GEN_EFF,P_MECH,POWER_TOTAL 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  pair,HH,Vair,rho_air,mu_air,kairopen 
c      DOUBLE PRECISION 
      CHARACTER*80      PARNAM(COMPAR),ZANAM(COMZA),ZDNAM(COMZD) 
      CHARACTER*100     K_PAR(9),K_STAT(1),KMEDDS(6) 
      CHARACTER*500     K_LIG(14), K_BET, KOMDSC,K_INP,K_GRAF 
      EXTERNAL          COMB_PRO,COMINF 
      INCLUDE 'THERPROP.INI' 
C==================================================================
===== 
      GOTO (100,200,1,400,400,200) FKOMP 
 1    RETURN 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component name 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  100 CONTINUE 
      KOMTY    = 'STIRLING_2' 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component characteristics 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  200 CONTINUE 
C Component name 
      KOMTY    = 'STIRLING_2' 
C Number of nodes 
      ANTKN    =  4 
C Number of parameters 
      ANTPK    =  13 
C Number of equations excluding ZA's 
      ANTLK    =  2 
C Number of ZA'S 
      ANTEX    =  5 
C Number of mass flows on side one 
      ANTM1    =  2 
C Number of mass flows on side two 
C     ANTM2    =  2 
C Media type 
   
      MEDIE(1) =  anyflu$ 
      MEDIE(2) =  anyflu$ 
      MEDIE(3) =  power$ 
      MEDIE(4) =  heat$ 
 
C Number of unspecified media 
      ANTME    =  2 
 
==PAGE:117==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
116 
 
C Specification of media 
 
      VARME(1) =  node1$ 
      VARME(2) =  node1$ 
C Number of computed compounds 
      ANTEL(1) =  0 
      ANTEL(2) =  0 
 
 
c Names of additional parameters 
      ZANAM(1)='ETAPCY [-]' 
      ZANAM(2)='Q HIGH   [kW]' 
      ZANAM(3)='eff_TOTAL  ' 
      ZANAM(4)='power to grid ' 
      ZANAM(5)='IRRADIATION [W/M2]' 
 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.6) GOTO 600 
***   FKOMP = 3 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component equations. All in residual form. 
C  Do not include the conservation laws, since these are treated 
C  automatically by DNA. 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  400 CONTINUE 
C  
C     User inputs      
 
      DPP_COOL = PAR(1) 
      T_HEATERWALL = PAR(2) 
      DELTAT_HIGH = PAR(3) 
      DELTAT_LOW = PAR(4) 
      RV = PAR(5) 
      EPSILON2 = PAR(6) 
      ETAMECH = PAR(7) 
      V_w=PAR(8) 
      T_sky=PAR(9) 
      T_a=PAR(10) 
      IRR=PAR(11)/1000 
c          {kW/M2}  
      U_supp_ratio=PAR(12) 
      N_UNITS=PAR(13) 
 
 
 
      D_abs=1.2 
      Tracking_power_pu=0.060     
c "40-100 [W]" 
      D=10.57 
      C=2793 
 
      PI=3.1415926 
      BOLTZ=5.670373D-8   
C               {W m2 k-4} 
 
      A_col=D**2/4*PI 
      APP_TOTAL=D**2/4*PI*N_UNITS  
==PAGE:118==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
117 
 
 
c {receiver}    
 
       pair=1 
      CALL STATES(pair,HH,T_a,Vair,S,X,U,1,3,9) 
      rho_air=1/Vair       
      mu_air=(-3.412E-11)*((T_a+273.15)**2)+(6.8709E-
8)*(T_a+273.15) 
     $     +9.9579E-7 
      Re_w=rho_air*V_w*D_abs/mu_air 
      Nu_w=0.3*Re_w**0.6 
      kairopen=0.00065877+(9.7222E-5)*(T_a+273.15)+ 
     $     (-3.8258E-8)*(T_a+273.15)**2 
      h_w=Nu_w*kairopen/D_abs 
      U_cc=h_w/(1-U_supp_ratio) 
c      write(6,*)'Re_w ',Re_w 
c      write(6,*)'Nu_w ',Nu_w 
c      write(6,*)'h_w ',h_w 
c      write(6,*)'U_cc ',U_cc 
       
 
      GEN_EFF=0.95 
      CONC_EFF=0.851 
      abs=0.93  
      transmit=0.93 
      REC_EFF= abs*transmit-(U_cc*(T_HEATERWALL-T_a)+0.9*BOLTZ* 
     $ ((T_HEATERWALL+273)**4-
(T_sky+273)**4))/(IRR*1000*C*CONC_EFF) 
      
c      write(6,*)' REC EFF ',REC_EFF 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
C Calling states for cooling water 
      CALL STATES(P(1),H(1),T_WATERIN,V(1),S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(1)) 
      CALL STATES(P(2),H(2),T_WATEROUT,V(2),S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(2)) 
 
c hIGH GAS TEMPERATURE 
      T_HEATERGAS=T_HEATERWALL-DELTAT_HIGH 
 
C Low temperature of gas in cooler 
      T_COOLERWALL=T_WATERIN+0.66667*(T_WATEROUT-T_WATERIN) 
      T_COOLERGAS=T_COOLERWALL+DELTAT_LOW 
 
C  Elproduktion 
      zeta=(T_COOLERGAS+273.15)/(T_HEATERGAS+273.15) 
      gamma=1.375 
      ETAPCY=((1-RV**(1-gamma))-zeta*(RV**(gamma-1)-1))/((1-RV**(1-
gamma 
     $     ))+(1-zeta)*(1-epsilon2)) 
 
      QHIGH=IRR*APP_TOTAL*CONC_EFF*REC_EFF 
      QLOSS=QHIGH*(1-ETAMECH) 
      P_MECH=ETAPCY*(QHIGH-QLOSS) 
      QLOW=(QHIGH-QLOSS-P_MECH) 
       
==PAGE:119==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
118 
 
      POWER_TOTAL=(P_MECH*GEN_EFF-Tracking_power_pu*N_UNITS) 
      EFF_total=P_MECH/QHIGH*CONC_EFF*GEN_EFF*REC_EFF 
 
c      write(6,*)' EFF TOTAL ',EFF_total 
c      write(6,*)' POWER_TOTAL ',POWER_TOTAL 
 
      power_2grid=-E-POWER_TOTAL 
C Residuals 
      RES(1)=P(1)-DPP_COOL-P(2) 
      RES(2)=H(1)*MDOT(1)+H(2)*MDOT(2)+QLOW 
 
C User output residualS 
      RES(3)=ZA(1)-ETAPCY 
      RES(4)=ZA(2)-QHIGH 
      RES(5)=ZA(3)-EFF_total 
      RES(6)=ZA(4)-power_2grid 
      RES(7)=ZA(5)-IRR*1000 
 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.5) GOTO 500 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Solution check 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  500 CONTINUE 
      IF (MDOT(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(2).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (power_2grid.GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
C      IF (Q(1).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (P(1).LT.P(2)) GOTO 550 
      GOTO 9999 
  550 FBETI = .FALSE. 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Write component information 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  600 CONTINUE 
      KOMDSC =  
     $ 'Stirling engine' 
      K_LIG(1) = 'P2 =P1-DDP_H' 
      K_LIG(2) = 'P4 =P3-DDP_C' 
      K_LIG(3) = 'X_J(O2) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(4) = 'X_J(N2) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(5) = 'X_J(CO2) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(6) = 'X_J(NO) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(7) = 'X_J(H2O) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(8) = 'X_J(SO2) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(9) = 'X_J(NO2) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(10) = 'X_J(Ar) = XPRO(M1,M2,X_J)' 
      K_LIG(11) = 'Q_loss = f_loss*Q_high' 
      K_LIG(12) = 'W_Stirling = eta_pc0*(Q_high-Q_loss)' 
      K_LIG(13) = 'Q_low = (Q_high-Q_loss-W_Stirling)' 
      K_LIG(14) = 'LAMBDA = (MDOT(1)/MDOT(2))/AFMIN' 
 
      K_PAR(1) = 'DPP' 
==PAGE:120==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
119 
 
      K_PAR(2) = 'LAMBDA' 
      K_PAR(3) = 'Electric eff.' 
      K_PAR(4) = 'Cooling/heating eff.' 
      K_PAR(5) = 'Loss eff.' 
      K_PAR(6) = 'Loss eff.' 
      K_PAR(7) = 'Loss eff.' 
      K_PAR(8) = 'Loss eff.' 
      K_PAR(9) = 'Loss eff.' 
 
      K_BET = 'MDOT1\\gt0 $ MDOT2\\gt0 $ MDOT3\\lt0 $ Q4\\lt0 $ '// 
     $     'P1\\gtP3 $ AF\\gtAFMIN' 
       
      K_MED(1) = MEDIE(1) 
      K_MED(2) = MEDIE(2) 
      K_MED(3) = MEDIE(3) 
      K_MED(4) = MEDIE(4) 
      K_MED(5) = MEDIE(5) 
      K_MED(6) = MEDIE(6) 
      K_MED(7) = MEDIE(7) 
 
      KMEDDS(1)= 'Air' 
      KMEDDS(2) = 'Fuel' 
      KMEDDS(3) = 'Combustion products' 
      KMEDDS(4) = 'Electricity' 
      KMEDDS(5) = 'Heat loss' 
      KMEDDS(6) = 'Heat production' 
 
      CALL COMINF(KOMTY,KOMDSC,ANTKN,ANTPK,ANTLK,1, 
     $     K_MED,K_PAR,K_LIG,K_BET,KMEDDS,K_STAT,K_INP,K_GRAF) 
      GOTO 9999 
C 
 9999 CONTINUE 
      RETURN 
      END

PTSC DNA MODEL 
 
*******************************************************************
**** 
      SUBROUTINE PTSC_SG(KOMTY,ANTLK,ANTEX,ANTKN,ANTPK,ANTM1, 
     :                    MEDIE,ANTME,VARME, 
     :                    MDOT,P,Q,H,ZA,PAR,RES,PARNAM,ZANAM, 
     $     
KCOMDS,KOMDSC,KMEDDS,K_PAR,K_LIG,K_STAT,K_BET,k_inp,K_GRAF) 
 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C PTSC_SG is a model for a steam-generator parabolic trough solar 
colector.  
C   
C 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
CA FKOMP - INPUT  - Flag with the value: 
CA                     1: Initialize the component. 
CA                     2: Initialize with actual system. 
CA                     3: Fluid composition calculation (constant). 
CA                     4: Find residuals. 
CA                     5: Find residuals and check variables. 
CA                     6: Output information about component. 
CA MDOT  - INPUT  - Massflows from nodes. 
CA P     - INPUT  - Pressure in nodes. 
CA Q     - INPUT  - Exchanged heat. 
CA PAR   - INPUT  - Parameters of the component. 
CA KOMTY - OUTPUT - Component name. 
CA ANTPK - OUTPUT - Number of parameters for the component. 
CA ANTLK - OUTPUT - Number of equations in the component. 
CA ANTEX - OUTPUT - Number of independent equations in the 
component. 
CA ANTED - OUTPUT - Number of differential independent equations. 
CA ANTKN - OUTPUT - Number of nodes connected to the component. 
CA ANTM1 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the first conservation 
of 
CA                  mass equation. 
CA ANTM2 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the second. 
CA DYCOM - OUTPUT - Type of conservation equations (static or 
dynamic 
CA                  mass and internal energy on side 1 and 2 
respectively; 
CA                  and dynamic solid internal energy). 
CA MEDIE - IN/OUT - Media (fluid) of the connected nodes. 
CA                  The values mean : 
CA                     99    : Water. 
CA                     300   : Heat. 
CA ANTME - OUTPUT - Number of fluids with variable composition. 
CA RES   - OUTPUT - Residuals for the component. 
C 
CL DP    Pressure loss through heat exchanger. 
==PAGE:122==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
121 
 
CL K_PAR Parameter description. 
CL K_LIG Equation description. 
CL K_BET Condition description. 
CL K_MED Media description. 
C 
CP Programmer : Nicolás Cobos Ullvius 
CP              Thermal Energy, DTU, Denmark. 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C  Including the common "environment" 
C 
      INCLUDE 'ENVIRO.INI' 
C 
C  Parameter variables 
C 
      INTEGER           ANTLK, ANTKN, MEDIE(3), ANTPK,ANTEX, 
     :                  ANTM1, ANTME, VARME(2) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  RES(10), MDOT(2), P(2),H(2),Q(1),PAR(7), 
     $ ZA(8) 
      CHARACTER*80      KOMTY,PARNAM(7),ZANAM(COMZA) 
C 
C  Local variables 
C      
      INTEGER           KK,ROWS 
      INTEGER           LL 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
D_ri,D_ro,D_ci,D_co,epsilon_r,epsilon_c,k_c,k_r, 
     $ 
boltz,aperture,reflectivity,intercept,transmissivity,absortivity, 
     $ K,aoi,eff_opt,P_mgas,manifold_loss,V_w,T_a,p_in,T_in,T_out, 
     $ Irrad_b,L,T_sky,A_coll,U_L,PI,T_ROM 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
rho_m1,v_m1,l_1,Re_1,DELTAp_L,rough_rel,f_Liq, 
     $ FF_LIQ(2) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
DP,Psat,V(2),T(2),Hliq,Tsat,Vliq,Xliq,Hvap,Vvap, 
     $ Xvap,Tfm1,Tfm3,T_rom1,pfm1,pfm3,Vfm1,x_1,mu_m1,k_1,Pr_1, 
     $ f_1,h_1,U_1,Vfm3,rho_m3,mu_m3,k_3,Pr_3  
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
DELTAevap,Pcrit,P_n,m,Fp,G,Bo,l_2,x_2,sec,qu, 
     $ quality_step,h_L(20),h_B,X_tt(20),FF(20),SS(20),h_2sum,U_2, 
     $ 
T_fm2,T_rom2,h_2avg,h_22avg,T_rom3,l_3,x_3,v_m3,Re_3,f_3,h_3,U_3, 
     $ 
pair,Hair,Vair,mu_air,k_air,Pr_air,rho_air,Re_w,Nu_w,kairopen,h_w 
     $      
      DOUBLE PRECISION  
T_ci,T_co,Q_losspu,T_mgas,P_mgas_mmHg,lambda, 
     $     
gamma,B,airk,k_effgas,FF_VAP(2),f_vap,DELTAp_vap,V_L,rho_L, 
     $     mu_L,k_L,Pr_L,V_G,rho_G,mu_G,k_G,Pr_G 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  TX,S,X,U,HH,N,ETA,PRANDT 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  sigma,DELTAp_L2ph_pu,E(20),F(20),HN(20), 
     $     rho_H(20),Fr(20),We(20),PHI(20),DELTAp_fric,DELTAp_mom, 
     $     DELTAp_2ph,Fr2(20),f_Liq2ph,h_11,h_33 
      CHARACTER*100     KMEDDS(3),kcomds 
      CHARACTER*100     K_PAR(1),K_STAT(1) 
==PAGE:123==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
122 
 
      CHARACTER*100     K_LIG(1) 
      CHARACTER*500     K_BET, KOMDSC,K_INP,K_GRAF 
C      character*500     mulspc,t 
C==================================================================
===== 
      GOTO (100,200,1,400,400,200) FKOMP 
 1    RETURN 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component name 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  100 CONTINUE 
      KOMTY    = 'PTSC_SG' 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component characteristics 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  200 CONTINUE 
C Component name 
      KOMTY    = 'PTSC_SG' 
C Number of nodes 
      ANTKN    =  3 
C Number of parameters 
      ANTPK    =  7  
C Number of equations excluding ZA's 
      ANTLK    =  2 
C Number of ZA'S 
      ANTEX    =  8 
C Number of mass flows on side one 
      ANTM1    =  2 
C Media type 
      MEDIE(1) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(2) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(3) =  HEAT$ 
C Number of unspecified media 
      ANTME    =  2 
C Specification of media 
      VARME(1) =  NODE1$ 
      VARME(2) =  NODE2$ 
c Names of parameters 
      PARNAM(1)   = 'IRRADIATION [W/M2K]' 
      PARNAM(2)   = 'Angle incidence [DEG]' 
      PARNAM(3)   = 'WIND VELOCITY [M/S]' 
      PARNAM(4)   = 'AMBIENT TEMP  [C]' 
      PARNAM(5)   = 'SKY TEMP [C]' 
      PARNAM(6)   = 'NUMBER PARALLEL ROWS' 
      PARNAM(7)   = 'LENGTH' 
 
 
c Names of additional parameters 
      ZANAM(1)='PSAT [BAR]' 
      ZANAM(2)='T_rom1   [C]' 
      ZANAM(3)='T_rom2   [C] ' 
      ZANAM(4)='T_rom3   [C]  ' 
      ZANAM(5)='T_co [C]' 
==PAGE:124==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
123 
 
      ZANAM(6)='U_L [W/M2K]' 
      ZANAM(7)='K [-]' 
      ZANAM(8)='IRRAD [W/M2]' 
 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.6) GOTO 600 
**    FKOMP = 3 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component equations. All in residual form. 
C  Do not include the conservation laws, since these are treated 
C  automatically by DNA. 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  400 CONTINUE 
C      
c ************************************************************** 
    
 
c constants and parameters 
      L=PAR(7) 
      aperture=2.5 
c  
      D_ri=0.033 
      D_ro=0.038  
      D_ci=0.084 
      D_co=0.09 
      epsilon_r=0.06 
      epsilon_c=0.86 
      k_c=0.035 
      k_r=60 
      boltz=5.670373E-8 
      PI=3.141592654 
       
      reflectivity=0.93 
      intercept=0.93 
      transmissivity=0.94 
      absortivity=0.94 
 
      P_mgas=0.0005 
       
C      write(6,*)' FLUID NUMBER ',NODE1$ 
       
      CALL STATES(P(1),H(1),T(1),V(1),S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(1)) 
      CALL STATES(P(2),H(2),T(2),V(2),S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(1)) 
      manifold_loss=0.2 
 
       
      aoi=PAR(2) 
      V_w=PAR(3) 
      T_a=PAR(4)+273 
      ROWS=PAR(6) 
      p_in=P(1)                                                   
      T_in=T(1)+273.15 
      T_out=T(2)+273.15 
      Irrad_b=PAR(1) 
      
      T_sky=PAR(5)+273.15 
==PAGE:125==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
124 
 
      A_coll=L*aperture 
       
C      write(6,*)' ROWS ',ROWS 
      
C OPTICAL EFFICIENCY 
 
      K=1-0.0000674*aoi**2+0.00000164*aoi**3-0.0000000251*aoi**4  
       eff_opt=reflectivity*intercept*transmissivity*absortivity*K 
 
C HEAT LOSS COEFFICIENT [W/M2-K] 
      U_L=ZA(6) 
 
 
 
C****** CALCULATION OF T_ROM ****** 
 
      Psat=ZA(1) 
 
       
 
      Xliq=0 
      Xvap=1 
      CALL STATES(Psat,Hliq,Tsat,Vliq,S,Xliq,U,1,6,MEDIE(1)) 
      Tfm1=(T_in+Tsat+273.15)/2 
      pfm1=(p_in+Psat)/2 
      CALL STATES(Psat,Hvap,Tsat,Vvap,S,Xvap,U,1,6,MEDIE(1)) 
      Tfm3=(T_out+Tsat+273.15)/2 
      pfm3=(P(2)+Psat)/2 
      DELTAevap=Hvap-Hliq 
 
 
      CALL STATES(pfm1,HH,Tfm1-273.15,Vfm1,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(1)) 
      rho_m1=1/Vfm1       
      call TRAPRO(mu_m1,k_1,Pr_1,pfm1,Tfm1-
273.15,Vfm1,X,MEDIE(1),1) 
 
 
 
      CALL STATES(pfm3,HH,Tfm3-273.15,Vfm3,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(1)) 
      rho_m3=1/Vfm3       
      call TRAPRO(mu_m3,k_3,Pr_3,pfm3,Tfm3-
273.15,Vfm3,X,MEDIE(1),1) 
 
 
 
c Temperature outer surface receiver in the liquid section 
      T_rom1=ZA(2)+273.15 
 
      l_1=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hliq-H(1))*1000/(eff_opt*Irrad_b*aperture 
     $ -U_L*D_ro*PI*(T_rom1-T_a)) 
      x_1=l_1/L 
 
      v_m1=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)/(rho_m1*D_ri**2/4*PI) 
      Re_1=rho_m1*v_m1*D_ri/mu_m1 
 
      rough_rel=0.000015/D_ri    
C 
{Absolute roughness of stainless steel (engineeringtoolbox)} 
      FF_LIQ(1)=0.02 
==PAGE:126==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
125 
 
      DO KK=1,5 
        FF_LIQ(2)=(-2*log10(rough_rel/3.7+2.51/ 
     $ (Re_1*(FF_LIQ(1)**0.5))))**(-2)     
C  Colebrook-White equation 
       FF_LIQ(1)=FF_LIQ(2) 
      ENDDO 
      f_Liq=FF_LIQ(2) 
  
       
      h_1=(f_Liq/8)*(Re_1-1000)*Pr_1/(1+12.7*(f_Liq/8)**(0.5)* 
     $ (Pr_1**(2/3)-1))*(k_1/D_ri) 
 
       
c  "Gnielinski correlation " 
      U_1=(D_ro/(h_1*D_ri)+D_ro*log(D_ro/D_ri)/(2*k_r))**(-1) 
 
       
      RES(4)=Tfm1+(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hliq-H(1))*1000/ 
     $     (PI*D_ro*l_1*U_1)-T_rom1 
C      write(6,*)' L_1 ',l_1 
C      write(6,*)' T_rom1 ',T_rom1 
 
 
 
 
 
 
c Temperature outer surface receiver in the 2-phase section 
      T_rom2=ZA(3)+273.15 
 
      l_2=((MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hvap-
Hliq)*1000/(eff_opt*Irrad_b*aperture 
     $ -U_L*D_ro*PI*(T_rom2-T_a))) 
      x_2=l_2/L 
 
      Pcrit=220.6 
      P_n=Psat/Pcrit 
      m=0.9-0.3*(P_n**0.15) 
      Fp=2.55*P_n**0.27*(9+1/(1-P_n**2))*P_n**2 
      G=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)/(D_ri**2/4*PI) 
      Bo=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hvap-Hliq)/(D_ri*PI*l_2)/(G*DELTAevap) 
      N=20 
      sec=l_2*0.99/N 
      qu=eff_opt*Irrad_b*sec*aperture-U_L*D_ro*PI*sec*(T_rom2-T_a) 
      quality_step=qu/((MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hvap-Hliq)*1000) 
      h_2sum=0 
       
 
      DO KK=1,N  
           
         Fr(KK)=(G**2)/(9.81*D_ri*rho_m1**2) 
c         write(6,*)' rhom1 ',rho_m1  
c         write(6,*)' fr ', Fr(KK) 
 
 
h_L(KK)=0.023*(G*(1-
quality_step*KK)*D_ri/mu_m1)**0.8*(Pr_1)**0.4 
     $ *k_1/D_ri 
 
==PAGE:127==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
126 
 
        if (Fr(KK).LT.4.0D-2)then 
         h_2sum=h_2sum+h_L(KK)*3.9*Fr(KK)**0.24*(quality_step*KK/ 
     $       (1-quality_step*KK))**0.64*(rho_m1/rho_m3)**0.5 
         
         else 
 
h_B=3800*((qu/(D_ri*PI*sec))/20000)**m*Fp  
 
 
X_tt(KK)=(rho_m3/rho_m1)**0.5*(mu_m1/mu_m3)**0.1* 
     $       ((1-quality_step*KK)/(quality_step*KK))**0.9 
 
 
FF(KK)=1+2.4E4*Bo**1.16+1.37*X_tt(KK)**(-0.86) 
        SS(KK)=1/(1+(1.15E-6)*FF(KK)**2* 
     $       (G*(1-quality_step*KK)*D_ri/mu_m1)**1.17) 
 
h_2sum=h_2sum+SS(KK)*h_B+h_L(KK)*FF(KK) 
        ENDIF 
      ENDDO 
      h_2avg=h_2sum/N 
C      write(6,*)' h2avg ',h_2avg 
      U_2=(D_ro/(h_2avg*D_ri)+D_ro*log(D_ro/D_ri)/(2*k_r))**(-1) 
      T_fm2=Tsat+273.15 
 
 
      RES(5)=T_fm2+(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(Hvap-
Hliq)*1000/(PI*D_ro*l_2*U_2) 
     $     -T_rom2 
C      write(6,*)' trom2 ',T_rom2   
C      write(6,*)' l2 ',l_2 
 
c      DO KK=1,N 
c         write(6,*)' h_L(KK) ',h_L(KK) 
c      enddo 
 
 
 
 
 
 
c Temperature outer surface receiver in the steam section 
      T_rom3=ZA(4)+273.15 
 
      l_3=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(H(2)-Hvap)*1000/(eff_opt*Irrad_b*aperture 
     $ -U_L*D_ro*PI*(T_rom3-T_a)) 
      x_3=l_3/L 
 
      v_m3=(MDOT(1)/ROWS)/(rho_m3*D_ri**2/4*PI) 
      Re_3=rho_m3*v_m3*D_ri/mu_m3 
 
 
      FF_VAP(1)=0.02 
      DO KK=1,5 
        FF_VAP(2)=(-2*log10(rough_rel/3.72+2.51/ 
     $ (Re_3*(FF_VAP(1)**0.5))))**(-2)     
C  Colebrook-White equation 
       FF_VAP(1)=FF_VAP(2) 
      ENDDO 
      f_vap=FF_VAP(2) 
 
       
      h_3=(f_vap/8)*(Re_3-1000)*Pr_3/(1+12.7*(f_vap/8)**(0.5)* 
==PAGE:128==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
127 
 
     $ (Pr_3**(2/3)-1))*(k_3/D_ri) 
 
c  "Gnielinski correlation " 
      U_3=(D_ro/(h_3*D_ri)+D_ro*log(D_ro/D_ri)/(2*k_r))**(-1) 
 
       
      RES(6)=Tfm3+(MDOT(1)/ROWS)*(H(2)-Hvap)*1000/(PI*D_ro*l_3*U_3) 
     $     -T_rom3 
C      write(6,*)' L_3 ',l_3 
C      write(6,*)' T_rom3 ',T_rom3 
 
 
       
 
 
c The weighted temperature on the outer surface of the receiver 
      T_ROM=T_rom1*x_1+T_rom2*x_2+T_rom3*x_3 
C     write(6,*)' T_ROM ',T_ROM 
 
 
 
 
c calculates the pressure drop in the liquid section and thus the 
saturation 
c pressure 
  
      DELTAp_L=(f_Liq*rho_m1*v_m1**2*l_1/D_ri/2)/100000 
 
      RES(3)=p_in-DELTAp_L-Psat 
 
c      write(6,*)' Psat ',Psat 
c      write(6,*)' tfm1 ',Tfm1 
c      write(6,*)' tfm3 ',Tfm3 
 
 
 
 
 
c Calculation of the heat loss to the ambient 
      pair=1 
      CALL STATES(pair,HH,T_a-273.15,Vair,S,X,U,1,3,9) 
      rho_air=1/Vair       
      mu_air=(-3.412E-11)*(T_a**2)+(6.8709E-8)*T_a+9.9579E-7 
      Re_w=rho_air*V_w*D_co/mu_air 
      Nu_w=0.3*Re_w**0.6 
      kairopen=0.00065877+(9.7222E-5)*T_a+(-3.8258E-8)*T_a**2 
      h_w=Nu_w*kairopen/D_co 
c      write(6,*)' kairopen ',kairopen 
C      write(6,*)' h_w ',h_w 
 
      T_co=ZA(5)+273.15 
 
      Q_losspu=PI*D_co*h_w*(T_co-T_a)+ 
     $     epsilon_c*PI*D_co*boltz*(T_co**4-T_sky**4) 
 
      T_ci=T_co+Q_losspu*log(D_co/D_ci)/(2*PI*k_c) 
       
      T_mgas=(T_ROM+T_ci)/2 
==PAGE:129==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
128 
 
      P_mgas_mmHg=P_mgas*750.0617              
C     "From model 2.pdf" 
      lambda=2.331E-10*T_mgas/(P_mgas_mmHg*2.32E-8) 
      gamma=1.37975268+(0.00017703)*T_mgas+(-4.2745E-7)*T_mgas**2+ 
     $     (2.0315E-10)*T_mgas**3 
      B=(2-1)/1*(9*gamma-5)/(2*(gamma+1)) 
      airk=0.00284939+(8.514E-5)*T_mgas+(-2.1952E-8)*T_mgas**2 
      k_effgas=airk/((D_ro/2)*log((D_ro+D_ci)/(2*D_ro))+ 
     $     B*lambda*((2*D_ro)/(D_ro+D_ci)+1))          
       
 
      RES(7)=((2*PI*k_effgas)/(log(D_ci/D_ro))*(T_ROM-T_ci)+ 
     $     (PI*D_ro*boltz*(T_ROM**4-T_ci**4))/ 
     $   (1/epsilon_r+(1-epsilon_c)*(D_ro/D_ci)/epsilon_c))-
Q_losspu 
 
       
      RES(8)=Q_losspu/(PI*D_ro*(T_ROM-T_a))-(1-manifold_loss)*U_L 
 
C      write(6,*)' U_L ',U_L 
 
 
 
 
 
C PRESSURE LOSS IN THE REMAINING PIPE LENGTH: 2-PHASE AND VAPOUR 
      
 
      DELTAp_vap=f_vap*rho_m3*v_m3**2*l_3/D_ri/2/100000 
C      write(6,*)' DELTAp_vap ',DELTAp_vap 
 
      CALL STATES(Psat,HH,Tsat-0.5,V_L,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(1)) 
      rho_L=1/V_L       
C      write(6,*)' rho L ',rho_L 
      call TRAPRO(mu_L,k_L,Pr_L,Psat,Tsat-0.5,V_L,X,MEDIE(1),0) 
      CALL STATES(Psat,HH,Tsat+0.5,V_G,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(1)) 
      rho_G=1/V_G   
C       write(6,*)' rho G ',rho_G 
      call TRAPRO(mu_G,k_G,Pr_G,Psat,Tsat+0.5,V_G,X,MEDIE(1),0) 
       
       
      sigma=0.11993071+(-0.00013089)*(Tsat+273.15)+ 
     $     (-9.0999E-8)*(Tsat+273.15)**2 
      DELTAp_L2ph_pu=f_liq*rho_m1*v_m1**2*l_2/N/D_ri/2/100000 
C      write(6,*)' sigma ',sigma 
C      write(6,*)' DELTAp_L2ph_pu ',DELTAp_L2ph_pu 
      DELTAp_fric=0  
 
      DO KK=1,N  
c "Friedel correlation" 
 
E(KK)=(1-
(quality_step*KK))**2+(quality_step*KK)**2*rho_L*f_vap/ 
     $        (rho_G*f_liq) 
 
F(KK)=(quality_step*KK)**0.78*(1-(quality_step*KK))**0.224 
 
HN(KK)=(rho_L/rho_G)**0.91*(mu_G/mu_L)**0.19*(1-
mu_G/mu_L)**0.7 
 
rho_H(KK)=((quality_step*KK)/rho_G+(1-
(quality_step*KK))/rho_L)**(-1) 
==PAGE:130==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
129 
 
 
Fr2(KK)=G**2/(9.81*D_ri*rho_H(KK)**2) 
 
We(KK)=G**2*D_ri/(sigma*rho_H(KK)) 
c         write(6,*)' fr2 ',Fr2(KK) 
c         write(6,*)' rhoH ',rho_H(KK) 
c         write(6,*)' X ',quality_step*KK 
        
PHI(KK)=E(KK)+3.24*F(KK)*HN(KK)/(Fr2(KK)**0.045*We(KK)**0.035) 
 
 
DELTAp_fric=DELTAp_fric+DELTAp_L2ph_pu*PHI(KK) 
      ENDDO 
C      write(6,*)' DELTAp_fric ',DELTAp_fric 
      DELTAp_mom=G**2*(1-1/rho_L)/100000 
C      write(6,*)' DELTAp_mom ',DELTAp_mom 
    
      DELTAp_2ph=DELTAp_fric+DELTAp_mom 
 
C      write(6,*)' DELTAp_2ph ',DELTAp_2ph 
    
      
      
c total pressure drop 
      DP=DELTAp_L+DELTAp_2ph+DELTAp_vap 
C      write(6,*)' DP ',DP 
 
      RES(1)    = P(1) - P(2) - DP 
      RES(2)=ROWS*(eff_opt*Irrad_b*A_coll-U_L*D_ro*PI*L*(T_ROM-
T_a)) 
     $ -Q(1)*1000 
       
 
 
c extra output 
      RES(9)=ZA(7)-K 
      RES(10)=ZA(8)-Irrad_b 
 
 
 
C 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.5) GOTO 500 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Solution check 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  500 CONTINUE 
      IF (MDOT(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (l_1.LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(2).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (Q(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (U_L.LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (aoi.LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (aoi.GT.90) GOTO 550 
      IF (Tsat.GT.T(2)) GOTO 550 
      GOTO 9999 
  550 FBETI = .FALSE. 
      GOTO 9999

-----

C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  600 CONTINUE 
      KCOMDS = 'Heat source' 
      KOMDSC = 'HEATSRC0 is a heat source with pressure loss given  
     $     in absolute terms' 
c      KOMFIG =  
      K_LIG(1) = 'Pressure loss $p_2 = p_1 - \\Delta p$' 
      K_PAR(1) = 'Pressure loss: $\\Delta p$ [bar]' 
      K_BET    = '$\\dot{m}_1 \\gt 0$\\\\ $\\dot{m}_2\\lt 0$\\\\ 
     $     $\\dot{Q} \\gt 0$' 
      KMEDDS(1) = 'Fluid inlet' 
      KMEDDS(2) = 'Fluid outlet'

     $'struc heatsource heatsrc0 1 2 301 1.0\\\\\n

     $addco t heatsource 2 100' 
 9999 CONTINUE 
      RETURN 
      END

                                  "Balance equations for each segment" 
 
"Calculates the mass flow and temperature variation in the segment"

1/R_M[1]=C_M*(Diff[1]*0,018/(P_aM[1]*8,314*T_m[1])) 
Diff[1]=1,19*10^(-4)*(T_m[1]^1,75/(P_m[1])) 
{P_aM[1]=20000*x} 
{P_aM[1]=100000*x} 
P_aM[1]=(x*P_F[1]-x*P_P[1])/ln(x*P_F[1]/(x*P_P[1])) 
x=800*10^(-6) 
1/R_pf[1]=C_pf*(0,018*P_m[1]/(1,08*10^(-5)*8,314*T_m[1])) 
C_K=15,18*10^(-4) 
C_M=5,1*10^3 
C_pf=12,97*10^(-11)

water with UNITS conversion" 
 
log10(P_wm[1]*760/101300)=8,07131-1730,63/(233,426+(T_Fm[1]-273)) 
P_Fm[1]=P_wm[1]*(1-x_s)

"Heat transfer balance"

{IF (Re<2100) THEN} 
{(h_F)*d_i/k_F=1,62*(Re_F*Pr_F*d_i/L)^0,33} 
{ Nu_F=1,62*(Re_F*Pr_F*d_i/L)^0,33} 
{(h_F[6])*d_i/k_F[6]=0,042*Re_F[6]^0,59*Pr_F[6]^0,33} 
(h_F[6])*d_i/k_F[6]=4,36+0,036*Re_F[6]*Pr_F[6]*d_i*L/(1+0,0011*(Re_F[6]*Pr_F[6]*d_i*L)^0,8) 
{ELSE} 
{h_F*d_i/k_F=0,023*Re_F^0,8*Pr_F^0,33} 
{END IF}

L)^0,8) 
{ELSE}

DCMD DNA MODEL 
 
*******************************************************************
**** 
      SUBROUTINE DCMD(KOMTY,ANTLK,ANTKN,ANTPK,ANTM1,ANTM2,ANTEX, 
     :                    MEDIE,ANTME,VARME, 
     :                    MDOT,P,Q,H,ZA,PAR,RES,PARNAM,ZANAM, 
     $     
KCOMDS,KOMDSC,KMEDDS,K_PAR,K_LIG,K_STAT,K_BET,k_inp,K_GRAF) 
 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C Direct Contact Membrane Distillation of sea water (35g/Kg). 
c It´s a limited model built based on the results from a model in 
EES.  
c Here the permeate side flow conditions are  
c constant and the feed side can vary its temperature-in  between 
the limits: 
c 70<T [C]<90 .The mass flow in will be divided between the number 
of units  
c needed. 
C 
c NOTE: Since there is no sea water media defined, clear water have 
been used 
c and  the outlet temperatures had to be defined by a correlation 
leading a  
c virtual heat imbalance which represents this difference. That´s 
why the heat 
c in this component is not zero.  
C 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
CA FKOMP - INPUT  - Flag with the value: 
CA                     1: Initialize the component. 
CA                     2: Initialize with actual system. 
CA                     3: Fluid composition calculation (constant). 
CA                     4: Find residuals. 
CA                     5: Find residuals and check variables. 
CA                     6: Output information about component. 
CA MDOT  - INPUT  - Massflows from nodes. 
CA P     - INPUT  - Pressure in nodes. 
CA Q     - INPUT  - Exchanged heat. 
CA PAR   - INPUT  - Parameters of the component. 
CA KOMTY - OUTPUT - Component name. 
CA ANTPK - OUTPUT - Number of parameters for the component. 
CA ANTLK - OUTPUT - Number of equations in the component. 
CA ANTEX - OUTPUT - Number of independent equations in the 
component. 
CA ANTED - OUTPUT - Number of differential independent equations. 
CA ANTKN - OUTPUT - Number of nodes connected to the component. 
CA ANTM1 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the first conservation 
of 
==PAGE:156==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
155 
 
CA                  mass equation. 
CA ANTM2 - OUTPUT - Number of massflows in the second. 
CA DYCOM - OUTPUT - Type of conservation equations (static or 
dynamic 
CA                  mass and internal energy on side 1 and 2 
respectively; 
CA                  and dynamic solid internal energy). 
CA MEDIE - IN/OUT - Media (fluid) of the connected nodes. 
CA                  The values mean : 
CA                     99    : Water. 
CA                     300   : Heat. 
CA ANTME - OUTPUT - Number of fluids with variable composition. 
CA RES   - OUTPUT - Residuals for the component. 
C 
CL DP    Pressure loss through heat exchanger. 
CL K_PAR Parameter description. 
CL K_LIG Equation description. 
CL K_BET Condition description. 
CL K_MED Media description. 
C 
CP Programmer : Nicolás Cobos Ullvius 
CP              Thermal Energy, DTU, Denmark. 
C******************************************************************
***** 
C 
C  Including the common "environment" 
C 
      INCLUDE 'ENVIRO.INI' 
C 
C  Parameter variables 
C 
      INTEGER           ANTLK, ANTKN, MEDIE(5), ANTPK, ANTEX, 
     :                  ANTM1,ANTM2, ANTME, VARME(4) 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  RES(11), MDOT(4), P(4),H(4), Q(1), 
PAR(1),ZA(4) 
      CHARACTER*80      KOMTY,PARNAM(1),ZANAM(COMZA) 
C 
C  Local variables 
C 
      INTEGER           KK,N_UNITS 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  DPF,DPP,V,S,X,U,d_o,L,N,PI,M1 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  TP_out,TF_out,JM,JMTOT, T3,T1,HF_out,HP_out 
      DOUBLE PRECISION  dx,TF70,TF75,TF80,TF85,TF90, 
     $     TP70,TP75,TP80,TP85,TP90, 
     $     JM70,JM75,JM80,JM85,JM90, 
     $     DPF70,DPF75,DPF80,DPF85,DPF90, 
     $     DPP70,DPP75,DPP80,DPP85,DPP90, 
     $     MAXTHP_P90,MAXTHP_P85,MAXTHP_P80,MAXTHP_P75,MAXTHP_P70, 
     $     MAXTHP_F90,MAXTHP_F85,MAXTHP_F80,MAXTHP_F75,MAXTHP_F70, 
     $     MAXTHP_P,MAXTHP_F,LEP 
 
 
      CHARACTER*100     KMEDDS(3),kcomds 
      CHARACTER*100     K_PAR(1),K_STAT(1) 
      CHARACTER*100     K_LIG(1) 
      CHARACTER*500     K_BET, KOMDSC,K_INP,K_GRAF 
C      character*500 mulspc,t 
==PAGE:157==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
156 
 
C==================================================================
===== 
      GOTO (100,200,1,400,400,200) FKOMP 
 1    RETURN 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component name 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  100 CONTINUE 
      KOMTY    = 'DCMD' 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Component characteristics 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  200 CONTINUE 
C Component name 
      KOMTY    = 'DCMD' 
C Number of nodes 
      ANTKN    =  5 
C Number of parameters 
      ANTPK    =  0 
C Number of equations excluding ZA's 
      ANTLK    =  7 
C Number of ZA'S 
      ANTEX    =  4 
C Number of mass flows on side one 
      ANTM1    =  4 
C Number of mass flows on side two 
      ANTM2    =   0 
C Media type 
      MEDIE(1) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(2) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(3) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(4) =  ANYFLU$ 
      MEDIE(5) =  HEAT$ 
C Number of unspecified media 
      ANTME    =  4 
C Specification of media 
      VARME(1) =  NODE1$ 
      VARME(2) =  NODE1$ 
      VARME(3) =  NODE3$ 
      VARME(4) =  NODE3$ 
c Names of parameters  
C      PARNAM(1)   = 'Pressure loss' 
c Names of additional parameters 
      ZANAM(1)='WATER DISTILLATED ' 
      ZANAM(2)='N_UNITS ' 
      ZANAM(3)='MAXTHP FEED ' 
      ZANAM(4)='MAXTHP PERM ' 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.6) GOTO 600

      GOTO 9999

         ENDIF 
      ENDIF 
 
      IF (T1.GT.85)THEN  
         IF (T1.LE.90.01)THEN 
C         write(6,*)' 8590 ',T1 
 
         dx=(T1-85)/5          
         
         TF85=52448*M1**4 - 31158*M1**3 + 6776.8*M1**2 - 425.85*M1  
     $        + 33.164 
         TF90=29138*M1**4 - 21873*M1**3 + 5588*M1**2 - 364.42*M1  
     $        + 32.054         
          
         TP85=52448*M1**4 - 18104*M1**3 - 110.14*M1**2 + 640.06*M1  
     $        + 21.86 
         TP90=72844*M1**4 - 27409*M1**3 + 1246.8*M1**2 + 598.36*M1  
     $        + 23.573         
          
         JM85=24242*M1**4 - 11803*M1**3 + 1579.1*M1**2 + 63.092*M1  
     $        + 0.6213 
         JM90=23077*M1**4 - 12104*M1**3 + 1696*M1**2 + 72.98*M1 + 
0.8208 
         
         DPF85=-520.69*M1**4 + 301.62*M1**3 - 64.206*M1**2 + 
7.4342*M1  
     $        - 0.0172 
         DPF90=-443.18*M1**4 + 274.58*M1**3 - 61.703*M1**2 + 
7.2733*M1  
     $        - 0.0148 
        
         DPP85=-483.39*M1**4 + 221*M1**3 - 31.299*M1**2 + 0.1408*M1  
     $        + 0.4726 
         DPP90=-445.51*M1**4 + 210.09*M1**3 - 30.671*M1**2 + 
0.1096*M1  
     $        + 0.4737 
 
==PAGE:162==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
161 
 
         MAXTHP_F85=32167832.17*M1**4 -245532.2455*M1**3  
     $        -3273473.193*M1**2 + 371137.3737*M1 + 102831 
         MAXTHP_F90=25320512.82*M1**4 + 3018842.269*M1**3  
     $        -4002648.601*M1**2+ 418336.1111*M1 + 101697 
 
         MAXTHP_P85=-50611888.11*M1**4 + 23407731.16*M1**3 - 
     $        3491826.923*M1**2 + 37195*M1 + 144963 
         MAXTHP_P90=-46853146.85*M1**4 + 22177156.18*M1**3  
     $        -3405839.161*M1**2 + 32770.74592*M1 + 145101.4825 
 
         TF_out=TF85+(TF90-TF85)*dx 
         TP_out=TP85+(TP90-TP85)*dx 
         JM=JM85+(JM90-JM85)*dx 
         DPF=DPF85+(DPF90-DPF85)*dx 
         DPP=DPP85+(DPP90-DPP85)*dx 
         MAXTHP_P=MAXTHP_P85+(MAXTHP_P90-MAXTHP_P85)*dx 
         MAXTHP_F=MAXTHP_F85+(MAXTHP_F90-MAXTHP_F85)*dx 
C         write(6,*)'MAXTHP_P  ',MAXTHP_P 
C         write(6,*)'MAXTHP_F  ',MAXTHP_F 
         ENDIF 
      ENDIF   
 
      IF (T1.GT.90.01)THEN 
C         write(6,*)' OUT OF RANGE ',T1 
         GOTO 550 
         TF_out=-9999 
         TP_out=-9999 
         JM=-9999 
         DPF=-9999 
         DPP=-9999 
      ENDIF 
 
       IF (T1.LE.69.99)THEN 
         write(6,*)' OUT OF RANGE ',T1 
         GOTO 550 
         TF_out=-9999 
         TP_out=-9999 
         JM=-9999 
         DPF=-9999 
         DPP=-9999 
      ENDIF 
 
 
c      write(6,*)' Dx ',dx 
c      write(6,*)' TF_out ',TF_out 
c      write(6,*)' TP_out ',TP_out 
c      write(6,*)' JM ',JM 
c      write(6,*)' DPF ',DPF 
c      write(6,*)' DPP ',DPP 
 
c pressure drop 
      RES(1)=P(1)-P(2)-DPF 
      RES(2)=P(3)-P(4)-DPP 
 
C LEP control 
      
      LEP=1.85  
 
==PAGE:163==
Design of polygeneration system based on solar power and solid oxide cells 
 
 
162 
 
      MAXTHP_F=MAXTHP_F/1E5+(P(2)-1.013) 
      MAXTHP_P=MAXTHP_P/1E5+(P(4)-1.013) 
       
 
c define outlet temperatures 
      CALL STATES(P(2),HF_out,TF_out,V,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(3)) 
      RES(3)=H(2)-HF_out 
      CALL STATES(P(4),HP_out,TP_out,V,S,X,U,1,3,MEDIE(3)) 
      RES(4)=H(4)-HP_out 
 
 
c calculate the total distilled water by all units 
      JMTOT=(JM/3600)*N*d_o*PI*L*N_UNITS 
 
      CALL STATES(P(3),H(3),T3,V,S,X,U,1,2,MEDIE(3)) 
 
c define permeate flow inlet conditions (constant) 
      RES(5)=25-T3       
      RES(6)=0.1*N_UNITS-MDOT(3) 
 
c outlet feed flow  
      RES(7)=MDOT(1)-JMTOT+MDOT(2) 
 
 
C     extra output results     
      RES(8)=ZA(1)-JMTOT 
      RES(9)=ZA(2)-N_UNITS 
      RES(10)=ZA(3)-MAXTHP_F 
      RES(11)=ZA(4)-MAXTHP_P 
 
C   
C 
       
        
C 
      IF (FKOMP.EQ.5) GOTO 500 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Solution check 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
  500 CONTINUE 
      IF (MDOT(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(2).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(3).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MDOT(4).GT.1D-10) GOTO 550 
      IF (MAXTHP_F.GT.LEP) GOTO 550 
      IF (MAXTHP_P.GT.LEP) GOTO 550 
C      IF (Q(1).LT.-1D-10) GOTO 550 
      GOTO 9999 
  550 FBETI = .FALSE. 
      GOTO 9999 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
C  Write component information (DOESN´T APPLY FOR DCMD) 
C------------------------------------------------------------------
----- 
==PAGE:164==

  600 CONTINUE 
      KCOMDS = 'Direct contact distillation membrane' 
      KOMDSC = 'HEATSRC0 is a heat source with pressure loss given  
     $     in absolute terms' 
c      KOMFIG =  
      K_LIG(1) = 'Pressure loss $p_2 = p_1 - \\Delta p$' 
      K_PAR(1) = 'Pressure loss: $\\Delta p$ [bar]' 
      K_BET    = '$\\dot{m}_1 \\gt 0$\\\\ $\\dot{m}_2\\lt 0$\\\\ 
     $     $\\dot{Q} \\gt 0$' 
      KMEDDS(1) = 'Fluid inlet' 
      KMEDDS(2) = 'Fluid outlet' 
      KMEDDS(3) = 'Heat inlet' 
      k_inp= 
     $'struc heatsource heatsrc0 1 2 301 1.0\\\\\n 
     $media 1 SIMPLE_AIR\\\\\n 
     $addco m heatsource 1 10 p 1 5\\\\\n 
     $addco t heatsource 1 50\\\\\n 
     $addco t heatsource 2 100' 
 9999 CONTINUE 
      RETURN 
      END
